## <a name="windows-server-2008-r2-attributes"></a><span data-ttu-id="fb422-1705">Atributos do Windows Server 2008 R2</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb422-1705">Windows Server 2008 R2 Attributes</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fb422-1706">Essa classe contém os seguintes atributos para o Windows Server 2008 R2:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb422-1706">This class contains the following attributes for Windows Server 2008 R2:</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="fb422-2069">Entrada</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb422-2069">Entry</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="fb422-2070">Valor</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fb422-2070">Value</span></span> |
